       Here is more information on the directives which may be included in a [1mlogrotate[0m configuration file:[m
[m
       [1mcompress[0m[m
              Old versions of log files are compressed with [1mgzip[0m(1) by default. See also [1mnocompress[0m.[m
[m
       [1mcompresscmd[0m[m
              Specifies which command to use to compress log files.  The default is [1mgzip[0m.  See also [1mcompress[0m.[m
[m
       [1muncompresscmd[0m[m
              Specifies which command to use to uncompress log files.  The default is [1mgunzip[0m.[m
[m
       [1mcompressext[0m[m
              Specifies which extension to use on compressed logfiles, if compression is enabled.  The default follows that of the configured compression command.[m
[m
       [1mcompressoptions[0m[m
              Command line options may be passed to the compression program, if one is in use.  The default, for [1mgzip[0m(1), is "-6" (biased towards high compression at the expense of speed).   If[m
              you use a different compression command, you may need to change the [1mcompressoptions[0m to match.[m
[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 113 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K       [1mcopy[0m   Make  a  copy of the log file, but don't change the original at all.  This option can be used, for instance, to make a snapshot of the current log file, or when some other utility[m
              needs to truncate or parse the file.  When this option is used, the [1mcreate[0m option will have no effect, as the old log file stays in place.[m
[m
       [1mcopytruncate[0m[m
              Truncate the original log file in place after creating a copy, instead of moving the old log file and optionally creating a new one.  It can be used when some  program  cannot  be[m
              told  to  close  its logfile and thus might continue writing (appending) to the previous log file forever.  Note that there is a very small time slice between copying the file and[m
              truncating it, so some logging data might be lost.  When this option is used, the [1mcreate[0m option will have no effect, as the old log file stays in place.[m
[m
       [1mcreate[0m [4mmode[24m [4mowner[24m [4mgroup[24m, [1mcreate[0m [4mowner[24m [4mgroup[24m[m
              Immediately after rotation (before the [1mpostrotate[0m script is run) the log file is created (with the same name as the log file just rotated).  [4mmode[24m specifies the mode  for  the  log[m
              file  in  octal  (the  same  as  [1mchmod[0m(2)), [4mowner[24m specifies the user name who will own the log file, and [4mgroup[24m specifies the group the log file will belong to. Any of the log file[m
              attributes may be omitted, in which case those attributes for the new file will use the same values as the original log file for the omitted attributes. This option  can  be  disâ€[m
              abled using the [1mnocreate[0m option.[m
[m
       [1mcreateolddir[0m [4mmode[24m [4mowner[24m [4mgroup[24m[m
              If the directory specified by [1molddir[0m directive does not exist, it is created. [4mmode[24m specifies the mode for the [1molddir[0m directory in octal (the same as [1mchmod[0m(2)), [4mowner[24m specifies the[m
              user name who will own the [1molddir[0m directory, and [4mgroup[24m specifies the group the [1molddir[0m directory will belong to. This option can be disabled using the [1mnocreateolddir[0m option.[m
[m
       [1mdaily[0m  Log files are rotated every day.[m
[m
       [1mdateext[0m[m
              Archive old versions of log files adding a date extension like YYYYMMDD instead of simply adding a number. The extension may be configured using the [1mdateformat[0m  and  [1mdateyesterday[0m[m
              options.[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 143 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K[m
       [1mdateformat[0m [4mformat_string[24m[m
              Specify  the extension for [1mdateext[0m using the notation similar to [1mstrftime[0m(3) function. Only %Y %m %d %H and %s specifiers are allowed.  The default value is -%Y%m%d except hourly,[m
              which uses -%Y%m%d%H as default value.  Note that also the character separating log name from the extension is part of the dateformat string. The system clock must be set past Sep[m
              9th  2001  for  %s  to  work  correctly.   Note  that  the datestamps generated by this format must be lexically sortable (i.e., first the year, then the month then the day. e.g.,[m
              2001/12/01 is ok, but 01/12/2001 is not, since 01/11/2002 would sort lower while it is later).  This is because when using the [1mrotate[0m option, logrotate sorts all rotated filenames[m
              to find out which logfiles are older and should be removed.[m
[m
       [1mdateyesterday[0m[m
              Use yesterday's instead of today's date to create the [1mdateext[0m extension, so that the rotated log file has a date in its name that is the same as the timestamps within it.[m
[m
       [1mdelaycompress[0m[m
              Postpone compression of the previous log file to the next rotation cycle.  This only has effect when used in combination with [1mcompress[0m.  It can be used when some program cannot be[m
              told to close its logfile and thus might continue writing to the previous log file for some time.[m
[m
       [1mextension[0m [4mext[24m[m
              Log files with [4mext[24m extension can keep it after the rotation.  If compression  is  used,  the compression extension (normally [1m.gz[0m) appears after [4mext[24m. For example you have a logfile[m
              named mylog.foo and want to rotate it to mylog.1.foo.gz instead of mylog.foo.1.gz.[m
[m
       [1mhourly[0m Log  files  are rotated every hour. Note that usually [4mlogrotate[24m is configured to be run by cron daily. You have to change this configuration and run [4mlogrotate[24m hourly to be able to[m
              really rotate logs hourly.[m
[m
       [1mifempty[0m[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 172 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K              Rotate the log file even if it is empty, overriding the [1mnotifempty[0m option ([1mifempty[0m is the default).[m
[m
       [1minclude[0m [4mfile_or_directory[24m[m
              Reads the file given as an argument as if it was included inline where the [1minclude[0m directive appears. If a directory is given, most of the files in  that  directory  are  read  in[m
              alphabetic  order  before  processing of the including file continues. The only files which are ignored are files which are not regular files (such as directories and named pipes)[m
              and files whose names end with one of the taboo extensions, as specified by the [1mtabooext[0m directive.[m
[m
       [1mmail[0m [4maddress[24m[m
              When a log is rotated out-of-existence, it is mailed to [4maddress[24m. If no mail should be generated by a particular log, the [1mnomail[0m directive may be used.[m
[m
       [1mmailfirst[0m[m
              When using the [1mmail[0m command, mail the just-rotated file, instead of the about-to-expire file.[m
[m
       [1mmaillast[0m[m
              When using the [1mmail[0m command, mail the about-to-expire file, instead of the just-rotated file (this is the default).[m
[m
       [1mmaxage[0m [4mcount[24m[m
              Remove rotated logs older than <count> days. The age is only checked if the logfile is to be rotated. The files are mailed to the configured address if [1mmaillast[0m and [1mmail[0m are  conâ€[m
              figured.[m
[m
       [1mmaxsize[0m [4msize[24m[m
              Log  files  are rotated when they grow bigger than [4msize[24m bytes even before the additionally specified time interval ([1mdaily[0m, [1mweekly[0m, [1mmonthly[0m, or [1myearly[0m).  The related [1msize[0m option is[m
              similar except that it is mutually exclusive with the time interval options, and it causes log files to be rotated without regard for the last  rotation  time.   When  [1mmaxsize[0m  is[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 201 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K              used, both the size and timestamp of a log file are considered.[m
[m
       [1mminsize[0m  [4msize[24m[m
              Log  files are rotated when they grow bigger than [4msize[24m bytes, but not before the additionally specified time interval ([1mdaily[0m, [1mweekly[0m, [1mmonthly[0m, or [1myearly[0m).  The related [1msize[0m option[m
              is similar except that it is mutually exclusive with the time interval options, and it causes log files to be rotated without regard for the last rotation time.  When  [1mminsize[0m  is[m
              used, both the size and timestamp of a log file are considered.[m
[m
       [1mmissingok[0m[m
              If the log file is missing, go on to the next one without issuing an error message. See also [1mnomissingok[0m.[m
[m
       [1mmonthly[0m[m
              Log files are rotated the first time [1mlogrotate[0m is run in a month (this is normally on the first day of the month).[m
[m
       [1mnocompress[0m[m
              Old versions of log files are not compressed. See also [1mcompress[0m.[m
[m
       [1mnocopy[0m Do not copy the original log file and leave it in place.  (this overrides the [1mcopy[0m option).[m
[m
       [1mnocopytruncate[0m[m
              Do not truncate the original log file in place after creating a copy (this overrides the [1mcopytruncate[0m option).[m
[m
       [1mnocreate[0m[m
              New log files are not created (this overrides the [1mcreate[0m option).[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 230 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K[m
       [1mnocreateolddir[0m[m
              [1molddir[0m directory is not created by logrotate when it does not exist.[m
[m
       [1mnodelaycompress[0m[m
              Do not postpone compression of the previous log file to the next rotation cycle (this overrides the [1mdelaycompress[0m option).[m
[m
       [1mnodateext[0m[m
              Do not archive  old versions of log files with date extension (this overrides the [1mdateext[0m option).[m
[m
       [1mnomail[0m Don't mail old log files to any address.[m
[m
       [1mnomissingok[0m[m
              If a log file does not exist, issue an error. This is the default.[m
[m
       [1mnoolddir[0m[m
              Logs are rotated in the same directory the log normally resides in (this overrides the [1molddir[0m option).[m
[m
       [1mnosharedscripts[0m[m
              Run [1mprerotate[0m and [1mpostrotate[0m scripts for every log file which is rotated (this is the default, and overrides the [1msharedscripts[0m option). The absolute path to the log file is passed[m
              as first argument to the script. If the scripts exit with error, the remaining actions will not be executed for the affected log only.[m
[m
       [1mnoshred[0m[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 260 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K              Do not use [1mshred[0m when deleting old log files. See also [1mshred[0m.[m
[m
       [1mnotifempty[0m[m
              Do not rotate the log if it is empty (this overrides the [1mifempty[0m option).[m
[m
       [1molddir[0m [4mdirectory[24m[m
              Logs are moved into [4mdirectory[24m for rotation. The [4mdirectory[24m must be on the same physical device as the log file being rotated, unless [1mcopy[0m,  [1mcopytruncate[0m  or  [1mrenamecopy[0m  option  is[m
              used. The [4mdirectory[24m is assumed to be relative to the directory holding the log file unless an absolute path name is specified. When this option is used all old versions of the log[m
              end up in [4mdirectory[24m.  This option may be overridden by the [1mnoolddir[0m option.[m
[m
       [1mpostrotate[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mpostrotate[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) after the log file is rotated. These directives may only[m
              appear  inside a log file definition. Normally, the absolute path to the log file is passed as first argument to the script. If [1msharedscripts[0m is specified, whole pattern is passed[m
              to the script.  See also [1mprerotate[0m. See [1msharedscripts[0m and [1mnosharedscripts[0m for error handling.[m
[m
       [1mprerotate[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mprerotate[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) before the log file is rotated and only if the  log  will[m
              actually  be  rotated.  These  directives  may only appear inside a log file definition. Normally, the absolute path to the log file is passed as first argument to the script.  If[m
              [1msharedscripts[0m is specified, whole pattern is passed to the script.  See also [1mpostrotate[0m.  See [1msharedscripts[0m and [1mnosharedscripts[0m for error handling.[m
[m
       [1mfirstaction[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mfirstaction[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) once before all log files  that  match  the  wildcarded[m
              pattern  are  rotated,  before prerotate script is run and only if at least one log will actually be rotated.  These directives may only appear inside a log file definition. Whole[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 291 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K              pattern is passed to the script as first argument. If the script exits with error, no further processing is done. See also [1mlastaction[0m.[m
[m
       [1mlastaction[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mlastaction[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) once after all log files that match the wildcarded  patâ€[m
              tern are rotated, after postrotate script is run and only if at least one log is rotated. These directives may only appear inside a log file definition. Whole pattern is passed to[m
              the script as first argument. If the script exits with error, just an error message is shown (as this is the last action). See also [1mfirstaction[0m.[m
[m
       [1mpreremove[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mpreremove[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) once just before removal of a log  file.   The  logrotate[m
              will pass the name of file which is soon to be removed. See also [1mfirstaction[0m.[m
[m
       [1mrotate[0m [4mcount[24m[m
              Log files are rotated [4mcount[24m times before being removed or mailed to the address specified in a [1mmail[0m directive. If [4mcount[24m is 0, old versions are removed rather than rotated.[m
[m
       [1msize[0m [4msize[24m[m
              Log  files are rotated only if they grow bigger then [4msize[24m bytes. If [4msize[24m is followed by [4mk[24m, the size is assumed to be in kilobytes.  If the [4mM[24m is used, the size is in megabytes, and[m
              if [4mG[24m is used, the size is in gigabytes. So [4msize[24m [4m100[24m, [4msize[24m [4m100k[24m, [4msize[24m [4m100M[24m and [4msize[24m [4m100G[24m are all valid.[m
[m
       [1msharedscripts[0m[m
              Normally, [1mprerotate[0m and [1mpostrotate[0m scripts are run for each log which is rotated and the absolute path to the log file is passed as first argument to the script. That means a sinâ€[m
              gle script may be run multiple times for log file entries which match multiple files (such as the [4m/var/log/news/*[24m example). If [1msharedscripts[0m is specified, the scripts are only run[m
              once, no matter how many logs match the wildcarded pattern, and whole pattern is passed to them.  However, if none of the logs in the pattern require rotating,  the  scripts  will[m
              not  be  run  at  all. If the scripts exit with error, the remaining actions will not be executed for any logs. This option overrides the [1mnosharedscripts[0m option and implies [1mcreate[0m[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 319 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K              option.[m
[m
       [1mshred[0m  Delete log files using [1mshred[0m -u instead of unlink().  This should ensure that logs are not readable after their scheduled deletion; this is off by default.  See also [1mnoshred[0m.[m
[m
       [1mshredcycles[0m [4mcount[24m[m
              Asks GNU [1mshred[0m(1) to overwrite log files [1mcount[0m times before deletion.  Without this option, [1mshred[0m's default will be used.[m
[m
       [1mstart[0m [4mcount[24m[m
              This is the number to use as the base for rotation. For example, if you specify 0, the logs will be created with a .0 extension as they are rotated from the  original  log  files.[m
              If you specify 9, log files will be created with a .9, skipping 0-8.  Files will still be rotated the number of times specified with the [1mrotate[0m directive.[m
[m
       [1msu[0m [4muser[24m [4mgroup[24m[m
              Rotate  log  files  set  under this user and group instead of using default user/group (usually root). [4muser[24m specifies the user name used for rotation and [4mgroup[24m specifies the group[m
              used for rotation.[m
[m
       [1mtabooext[0m [+] [4mlist[24m[m
              The current taboo extension list is changed (see the [1minclude[0m directive for information on the taboo extensions). If a + precedes the list of extensions, the current  taboo  extenâ€[m
              sion  list  is  augmented,  otherwise  it  is replaced. At startup, the taboo extension list contains .rpmsave, .rpmorig, ~, .disabled, .dpkg-old, .dpkg-dist, .dpkg-new, .cfsaved,[m
              .ucf-old, .ucf-dist, .ucf-new, .rpmnew, .swp, .cfsaved, .rhn-cfg-tmp-*[m
[m
       [1mweekly[0m Log files are rotated if the current weekday is less than the weekday of the last rotation or if more than a week has passed since the last rotation. This is normally the same  as[m
              rotating logs on the first day of the week, but it works better if [4mlogrotate[24m is not run every night.[m
[m
[7m Manual page logrotate(8) line 347 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[K[[[K66[K~~[K       [1myearly[0m Log files are rotated if the current year is not the same as the last rotation.[m
[m

                                  Default state file.[m

[2;1H[m
[3;1H[1mNAME[0m[m
[4;1H       logrotate â€ rotates, compresses, and mails system logs[m
[5;1H[m
[6;1H[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
[7;1H       [1mlogrotate[0m [[1m-dv[0m] [[1m-f[0m|[1m--force[0m] [[1m-s[0m|[1m--state[0m [4mfile[24m] [4mconfig_file[24m ..[m
[8;1H[m
[9;1H[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
[10;1H       [1mlogrotate[0m is designed to ease administration of systems that generate large numbers of log files.  It allows automatic rotation, compression, removal, and mailing of log files.  Each log[m
[11;1H       file may be handled daily, weekly, monthly, or when it grows too large.[m
[12;1H[m
[13;1H       Normally, [1mlogrotate[0m is run as a daily cron job.  It will not modify a log multiple times in one day unless the criterion for that log is based on the log's size and  [1mlogrotate[0m  is  being[m
[14;1H       run multiple times each day, or unless the [1m-f[0m or [1m--force[0m option is used.[m
[15;1H[m
[16;1H       Any  number  of  config  files  may be given on the command line. Later config files may override the options given in earlier files, so the order in which the [1mlogrotate[0m config files are[m
[17;1H       listed is important.  Normally, a single config file which includes any other config files which are needed should be used.  See below for more information on  how  to  use  the  [1minclude[0m[m
[18;1H       directive to accomplish this.  If a directory is given on the command line, every file in that directory is used as a config file.[m
[19;1H[m
[20;1H       If no command line arguments are given, [1mlogrotate[0m will print version and copyright information, along with a short usage summary.  If any errors occur while rotating logs, [1mlogrotate[0m will[m
[21;1H       exit with non-zero status.[m
[22;1H[m
[23;1H[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[24;1H[1;1HLOGROTATE(8)                                                                      System Administrator's Manual                                                                      LOGROTATE(8)[m
[2;1H[m
[3;1H[1mNAME[0m[m
[4;1H       logrotate â€ rotates, compresses, and mails system logs[m
[5;1H[m
[6;1H[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
[7;1H       [1mlogrotate[0m [[1m-dv[0m] [[1m-f[0m|[1m--force[0m] [[1m-s[0m|[1m--state[0m [4mfile[24m] [4mconfig_file[24m ..[m
[8;1H[m
[9;1H[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
[10;1H       [1mlogrotate[0m is designed to ease administration of systems that generate large numbers of log files.  It allows automatic rotation, compression, removal, and mailing of log files.  Each log[m
[11;1H       file may be handled daily, weekly, monthly, or when it grows too large.[m
[12;1H[m
[13;1H       Normally, [1mlogrotate[0m is run as a daily cron job.  It will not modify a log multiple times in one day unless the criterion for that log is based on the log's size and  [1mlogrotate[0m  is  being[m
[14;1H       run multiple times each day, or unless the [1m-f[0m or [1m--force[0m option is used.[m
[15;1H[m
[16;1H       Any  number  of  config  files  may be given on the command line. Later config files may override the options given in earlier files, so the order in which the [1mlogrotate[0m config files are[m
[17;1H       listed is important.  Normally, a single config file which includes any other config files which are needed should be used.  See below for more information on  how  to  use  the  [1minclude[0m[m
[18;1H       directive to accomplish this.  If a directory is given on the command line, every file in that directory is used as a config file.[m
[19;1H[m
[20;1H       If no command line arguments are given, [1mlogrotate[0m will print version and copyright information, along with a short usage summary.  If any errors occur while rotating logs, [1mlogrotate[0m will[m
[21;1H       exit with non-zero status.[m
[22;1H[m
[23;1H[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[24;1H...skipping...
              Run [1mprerotate[0m and [1mpostrotate[0m scripts for every log file which is rotated (this is the default, and overrides the [1msharedscripts[0m option). The absolute [7mpath[27m to the log file is passed[m
              as first argument to the script. If the scripts exit with error, the remaining actions will not be executed for the affected log only.[m
[m
       [1mnoshred[0m[m
              Do not use [1mshred[0m when deleting old log files. See also [1mshred[0m.[m
[m
       [1mnotifempty[0m[m
              Do not rotate the log if it is empty (this overrides the [1mifempty[0m option).[m
[m
       [1molddir[0m [4mdirectory[24m[m
              Logs are moved into [4mdirectory[24m for rotation. The [4mdirectory[24m must be on the same physical device as the log file being rotated, unless [1mcopy[0m,  [1mcopytruncate[0m  or  [1mrenamecopy[0m  option  is[m
              used. The [4mdirectory[24m is assumed to be relative to the directory holding the log file unless an absolute [7mpath[27m name is specified. When this option is used all old versions of the log[m
              end up in [4mdirectory[24m.  This option may be overridden by the [1mnoolddir[0m option.[m
[m
       [1mpostrotate[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mpostrotate[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) after the log file is rotated. These directives may only[m
              appear  inside a log file definition. Normally, the absolute [7mpath[27m to the log file is passed as first argument to the script. If [1msharedscripts[0m is specified, whole pattern is passed[m
              to the script.  See also [1mprerotate[0m. See [1msharedscripts[0m and [1mnosharedscripts[0m for error handling.[m
[m
       [1mprerotate[0m/[1mendscript[0m[m
              The lines between [1mprerotate[0m and [1mendscript[0m (both of which must appear on lines by themselves) are executed (using [1m/bin/sh[0m) before the log file is rotated and only if the  log  will[m
              actually  be  rotated.  These  directives  may only appear inside a log file definition. Normally, the absolute [7mpath[27m to the log file is passed as first argument to the script.  If[m
              [1msharedscripts[0m is specified, whole pattern is passed to the script.  See also [1mpostrotate[0m.  See [1msharedscripts[0m and [1mnosharedscripts[0m for error handling.[m
